A dark, swirling vortex opens to the southwest, and drags you through it. (vortex) Crossing a shaky causeway. (road). (North Eastern Arena.) The causeway shakes with the wind as time and erosion has slowly worn down the posts keeping it fastened to the two pillars. The causeway descends towards the northeast as it approaches the shorter pillar while the taller pillar to the west provides a birds eye view of the entire arena. A large wall of stone stands here, blocking passage to the west. Lord Ozreas al-Hamasa is riding on a massive warhorse. He wields a curved sabre in his left hand and a weathered silver shield in his right.
